 Generally, if there is any structure, tree, plant, etc
 in the house or around the house that increase negative energy, then according to Vastu Shastra, it is considered to be serious Vastushadh
 in vaastudosha ko dur kar ghar or jivan ko bure prabhaavon se bachaaya ja saktaa he or positive energy ko barkaar rakhaa ja saktaa he: If you keep a bouquet of fresh flowers in your drawingroom or decorate it, keep in mind that these are changed at the right time
 ho sake to inhen roj badalen
 According to Vastu Shastra, when these flowers wither then they start increasing negative energy in the house
 praaia: gharon main sahi chunaai or plastering na hone kiwajah se kamaron kii deevaaron par sillen paidaa hone lagati he
 According to Indian architecture it is not considered auspicious
 sillen se bani bhaddi akritiyaan negative energy ko badhaati he
 Therefore, it is suggested that such walls be repaired as soon as possible
 ghar ke angan main lage ped-paudhe agar suukh jaaen, to unhen turant hatwa den
 Not only do they look ugly, but these trees represent the end of life and increase negative energy
 interior decoration ke liye kuch aisi painting or kalakritiyon kaa istemaal kiya jaataa he, jo mritpraaya ped-paudhon or jeev-jantuon ke avasheshon se bane hote hai
 All these dead decorative artifacts and objects, except conch, CP, coral, are not considered auspicious from the point of view of Vastushastra
 isliye inkaa upyog karne bachein
 If there are scenes such as dry trees from the bedroom window and the main gate of the house, smoke emanating from the factory chimney, transformers etc
, then put curtains on the windows and doors to avoid them
 aise drishy nakaaratmakataa main vruddhi karte hai
 US President Barack Obamane has given huge amount of money to Pakistan
 unhone ek arab dollar (63 arab bhartiya rupee) pakistani fouj dwaara afghanistan main america fouj kii madad ke liye die
 On Friday night, Obama signed America's 2015 national defense budget
 yah ab tak kaa sabase bada salanaa bajet he or america raksha par kul 578 arab dollar kharch karegaa
 Out of this, there is a provision to give one billion dollars to Pakistan
 yah dhan ek tarah se pakistan america fouj par kiye gaye kharch kii adaayagi he
 Although there are many conditions on the allocation of this amount, the Defense Minister has the right to measure these conditions
 aisa kai varshon se ho rahaa he
 By the way, this money is given to Pakistan for action against terrorist gangs, but a large amount of it goes here and there
 afghanistan se america phujon ke hatane ke baad bhi pakistan ko yah raashi dene par abhi charchaa chal rahi he
 By law, the US Defense Minister is required to submit a report in the Parliament there about the us-pakistan bilateral treaty within the first 90 days
 is ek arab kii raashi main se pakistan ko 30 karod dollar tab tak nahin milenge jab tak raksha mantri sansad ko nahin bataaenge ki pakistan ne uttar wajiristaan main kya faujee karrwai kii he
 The Taliban of the Haqqani gang are active there and remain a threat to the Afghan government
 america sansad pakistan se is sambandh main kaaphi baaten puch sakati he

 pichley do saal kii tarah is saal bhi misacusets institute of technology ko pehla sthaan mila he
